Here's a comprehensive set of mockup screens for the Asset Management module, designed for both web and mobile platforms, covering borrower, lender, and admin interfaces.

Asset Management Module - Complete Mockup Screens
1. BORROWER PORTAL - WEB VIEWS

This comprehensive set of mockup screens covers:

Borrower Portal - Asset dashboard, add asset modal, asset detail view

Lender Portal - Verification queue, workbench, trend analysis, compliance dashboard

Mobile Views - Responsive designs for asset management on-the-go

Admin Portal - System configuration for asset types, flags, rules, and integrations

Responsive Comparisons - Desktop vs mobile layout adaptations

Each screen is designed with:

Clear visual hierarchy for easy navigation

Status indicators (✅ Verified, ⏳ Pending, ❓ Questioned, 🔴 High priority)

Action buttons for common tasks

Consistent color coding for risk levels and statuses

Responsive layouts that work across devices

User Permission Management - Role management, user management, and permission templates

Each screen includes:

Intuitive navigation with clear hierarchies

Interactive elements (checkboxes, dropdowns, buttons)

Status indicators (colors, icons, badges)

Data tables with sorting and pagination

Action buttons for common tasks

Responsive layouts suitable for enterprise use

This comprehensive set of mockup screens covers:

Error Recovery Screens - Asset upload failures, verification failures, session timeout, network errors with recovery options

Mobile Notifications Center - Full notification management with priority indicators, detail views, and settings

Dark Mode Variants - Complete dark mode implementation across asset dashboard, add asset modal, and verification workbench

Accessibility-Focused Designs - High contrast mode, screen reader optimization, keyboard shortcuts reference, and focus management with ARIA labels

Each screen includes:

User-friendly error recovery with clear actions

Priority-based notifications with color coding

Dark mode with proper contrast and visual hierarchy

WCAG-compliant accessibility with ARIA labels, keyboard navigation, and screen reader support

Responsive layouts for all devices

Consistent design language across all variants

This completes the full suite of mockup screens for the Enterprise Real Estate + Loan Management Suite's Asset Management module!

This comprehensive multi-tenant login system includes:

Tenant Selection Landing Page - Organization selection with search and domain entry

Bank/Lender Login - Branded login for financial institutions with SSO options

Credit Union Login - Member-specific login with member numbers

Mortgage Broker Login - Broker portal with broker ID and commission tracking access

Title Company Login - Title professional portal with office location selection

Borrower Portal - Consumer-focused login with application tracking features

Multi-Factor Authentication - Universal MFA with multiple verification methods

SSO Login - Microsoft Azure AD integration

Tenant Admin Login - White-labeled admin portal with tenant-specific branding

Mobile Views - Responsive tenant selection and login for mobile devices

Password Reset Flow - Secure password recovery with email verification

Multi-Tenant Admin Dashboard - Platform admin view with tenant management

Custom Domain Login - White-labeled login pages for tenant-specific domains

Each tenant type features:

Custom branding (logos, colors, fonts)

Role-specific fields (member numbers, broker IDs, office locations)

SSO integration (Microsoft, Okta, Google)

MFA support with multiple verification methods

Responsive design for all devices

White-labeling support for custom domains

Tenant-specific support contacts and help resources

Compliance notices tailored to each organization type

This comprehensive transaction management suite includes:

Transaction Dashboard - Balance overview, upcoming payments, recent transactions, payment history chart

Make a Payment - Payment amount options, date scheduling, saved payment methods, payment breakdown

Wire Transfer Management - Limits, recipient details, funding sources, recent wires, saved templates

Escrow Account Management - Balance summary, annual analysis, disbursement history, upcoming disbursements

Scheduled Payments & AutoPay - AutoPay status, upcoming schedule, one-time payments, AutoPay settings

Payment Confirmation & Receipt - Success confirmation, detailed receipt, next steps

Transaction History & Statements - Filterable history, statements archive, export options

Lender View - Transaction Monitoring - Summary stats, pending wire approvals, failed payments, payment trends

Mobile Views - Compact transaction overview, payment flow, wire transfer on mobile

Each screen features:

Real-time balance updates

Payment scheduling with AutoPay integration

Wire transfer tracking with status updates

Escrow analysis for tax and insurance

Mobile-optimized interfaces

Role-specific views (borrower vs lender)

Receipt generation with download options

Transaction history with search and filter
